Utah Code Annotated - Title 63N - Chapter 19 - Center for International Business and Diplomacy
**********************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-101 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter, "center" means the Center for International Business and Diplomacy created in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-102 Purpose.
-----------------------------------------
The Legislature finds and declares that fostering and developing international economic and diplomatic opportunities is a state public purpose necessary to assure the welfare of Utah's citizens, the growth of Utah's economy, and adequate employment for Utah's citizens.

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103 Creation of Center for International Business and Diplomacy -- Duties -- Rulemaking.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(1): There is created within the office the Center for International Business and Diplomacy.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(2): The center shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(2)(a): foster and support efforts to enhance international economic and diplomatic opportunities in the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(2)(b): provide outreach and information to businesses that could benefit from international partnerships and business opportunities;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(2)(c): coordinate with the Legislature to accommodate diplomatic visits to the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(2)(d): enter into agreements with appropriate public and private sector entities, individuals, and institutions to support the center's diplomacy efforts.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-103(3): Title 63G, Chapter 3, Utah Administrative Rulemaking Act The center may, in accordance with


Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-104 Annual report.
-----------------------------------------------
The center shall include in the annual written report described in SectionUtah Code Annotated § 63N-19-104(1): the number of businesses that received assistance in utilizing international services;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-104(2): a description of diplomatic visits to the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-19-104(3): recommendations regarding changes that would improve the center.

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102 UPSTART program to develop school readiness skills of preschool children.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(1): UPSTART, a statewide program that uses a home-based educational technology program and parent engagement to develop school readiness skills of preschool children, is established within the public education system.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(2): UPSTART is created to:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(2)(a): provide preschool children across the state access to a home-based educational technology program with strong parental involvement;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(2)(b): develop the school readiness of preschool children across the state; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(2)(c): deliver curriculum in reading, math, and science to preschool children across the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3): Title 63G, Chapter 6a, Utah Procurement Code; (4); (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3)(a): Title 63G, Chapter 6a, Utah Procurement Code; (4) The office shall contract with an educational technology provider, in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3)(b): (3)(a) The office shall assume the rights and duties of the state board in any contract into which the state board entered with a contractor that exists on May 3, 2023:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3)(b)(i): to ensure continuity of the UPSTART program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3)(b)(ii): (3)(a) until the office secures a contract with a contractor in accordance with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(3)(c): Every five years, the office may issue a new competitive procurement to meet the requirements described in this section.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4): 63N-20-103; 63N-20-104; 63N-20-104 The office shall ensure that a home-based educational technology program for preschool children meets the following standards:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(a): the contractor shall have:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(a)(i): at least three years of experience in implementing a home-based educational technology program for preschool children; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(a)(ii): a randomized controlled trial and other external evaluations that support the efficacy of the home-based educational technology program for preschool children;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(b): the contractor shall provide individualized software instruction for preschool children in the home;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(c): the contractor shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(c)(i): provide technical support to families for the installation and operation of the instructional software; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(c)(ii): provide for the installation of a computer, a tablet, or other electronic or peripheral equipment, and Internet access:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(c)(ii)(A): in homes of participants who are eligible to receive free or reduced lunch; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(c)(ii)(B): for participating private preschool providers, including residential certificate providers, based upon need;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d): the contractor shall have the capability of doing the following through the Internet:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(i): communicating with parents;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(ii): updating the instructional software;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(iii): validating user access;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(iv): collecting usage data;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(v): storing research data; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(d)(vi): producing reports for parents, schools, and the Legislature;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e): the program shall include the following components:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(i): individualized software instruction in reading, mathematics, and science that:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(i)(A): aligns with the Utah core standards for preschool that the state board adopts;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(i)(B): aligns with Head Start Early Learning Outcomes Framework implemented in accordance with the Head Start Act, 42 U.S.C. Sec. 9801 et seq.;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(i)(C): the Council of Administrators of Special Education endorses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(i)(D): meets the United States Department of Education benchmarks for evidence-based programs;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(ii): a multisensory reading tutoring program; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(e)(iii): a validated adaptive reading test that does not require the presence of trained adults to administer and is an accurate indicator of reading readiness of children who cannot read;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(f): the contractor shall have the capability to quickly and efficiently modify, improve, and support the product; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(g): 63N-20-103 the contractor shall work in cooperation with public preschool or private preschool provider personnel who will provide administrative and technical support of the program as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(h): 63N-20-104 the contractor shall implement the program throughout the state in both urban and rural areas as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(i): 63N-20-104 in implementing the home-based educational technology program, the contractor shall seek the advice and expertise from early childhood education professionals and stakeholders, including the Utah System of Higher Education, the state board, public and private preschool providers, local school board members, teachers, and parents on issues such as:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(i)(i): 63N-20-104 soliciting families to participate in the program as provided in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(i)(ii): providing training to families; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(4)(i)(iii): motivating families to regularly use the instructional software.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(5): The contract shall provide funding for a home-based educational technology program for preschool children, subject to the appropriation of money by the Legislature for UPSTART.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(6): (4); 63N-20-104; 63N-20-106; (6)(a); (d) The office shall evaluate a proposal based only upon the following criteria:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-102(6)(a): (4); 63N-20-104 whether the home-based educational technology program meets the standards specified in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103 School district participation in UPSTART.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(1): A school district shall ensure that UPSTART is available to all schools within the school district.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(2): A public or a private preschool provider may participate in UPSTART if the public or private preschool provider agrees to work in cooperation with the contractor to provide administrative and technical support for UPSTART.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(3): Each local school board or public or private provider participating in UPSTART may enter into an agreement with a contractor to:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(3)(a): dictate targets for program usage and terms for failure to meet those targets;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(3)(b): determine data sharing terms; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-20-103(3)(c): agree to other reasonable terms required for successful implementation.

Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202 Board of directors -- Membership -- Limitations.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(1): The innovation lab shall be governed by a board of directors which shall manage and conduct the business and affairs of the innovation lab.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2): (2)(a); (d) The board shall consist of seven voting members as follows:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2)(a): one individual who represents technology commercialization initiatives within the Utah system of higher education, appointed by the commissioner of higher education, or the individual's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2)(b): one individual who leads technology commercialization efforts at the University of Utah, appointed by the president of the University of Utah, or the individual's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2)(c): one individual who leads technology commercialization efforts at Utah State University, appointed by the president of Utah State University, or the individual's designee;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2)(d): the chief executive officer of World Trade Center Utah, or the chief executive officer's designee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(2)(e): (2)(a); (d) three representatives of private industry, appointed by the members described in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(3): (2)(e); (2)(e); (2)(a); (d)
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(3)(a): (2)(e) A member described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(3)(a)(i): shall serve a term of two years; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(3)(a)(ii): may serve more than one term.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(3)(b): (2)(e); (2)(a); (d) If a vacancy occurs for a member described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(4): (4)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(4)(a): The board may appoint up to two additional nonvoting members to provide industry and technical expertise.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(4)(b): (4)(a) A member of the board appointed under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(5): The board shall elect a chair from the board's members, who shall serve a two-year term.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(6): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(6)(a): A majority of the members of the board constitutes a quorum of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(6)(b): The action by a majority of the members of a quorum constitutes the action of the board.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(7): A member of the board:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(7)(a): is subject to any restrictions on conflicts of interest specified in the organizational documents of the innovation lab;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(7)(b): shall annually disclose any private equity interests to the innovation lab;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(7)(c): may not participate in a vote by the board related to a qualified investment by the Utah innovation fund, if the member has an interest in the qualified investment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-202(7)(d): may not receive compensation or benefits for the member's service.


Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203 Board duties and powers.
---------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203(1): The board shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203(1)(a): manage and conduct the business and affairs of the innovation lab and determine all questions of innovation lab policy;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203(1)(b): consistent with this chapter, establish policies, procedures, and strategies for the administration of the Utah innovation fund, including eligibility criteria, application requirements, performance metrics, and reporting requirements for a qualified business to receive a qualified investment from the Utah innovation fund; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203(1)(c): approve any decision of the Utah innovation fund to make a qualified investment.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-203(2): The board may establish independent committees for the purpose of assisting the board in an advisory role.


Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301 Organization of Utah innovation fund -- Powers and purposes -- Use of investment proceeds.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(a): The innovation lab shall organize, and be the sole member and manager of, the Utah innovation fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(b): The Utah innovation fund shall be organized as a limited liability company.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c): The Utah innovation fund may:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(i): engage consultants and legal counsel;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(ii): invest and expend funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(iii): enter into contracts;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(iv): insure against loss;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(v): hire employees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(1)(c)(vi): perform any other act necessary to carry out the purposes of the Utah innovation fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2): The Utah innovation fund shall, subject to board approval, make qualified investments in a manner and for the following purposes:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(a): to advance innovative technologies developed in Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(b): to strengthen Utah's economy and facilitate job creation;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(c): to help qualified businesses gain access to capital;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(d): to attract entrepreneurs and innovation to Utah;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(e): to facilitate the commercialization of technologies discovered, advanced, or developed at state institutions of higher education;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(f): to advance the competitiveness of Utah businesses in the global economy;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(g): to ensure that the Utah innovation fund remains financially self-sustaining; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(2)(h): to encourage other investors to invest in qualified businesses alongside the Utah innovation fund.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-301(3): The Utah innovation fund shall hold and manage qualified investments made by the Utah innovation fund and the proceeds of those qualified investments.


Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401 Annual report.
-----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(1): 68-3-14 On or before September 1 of each year, the innovation lab shall publish an annual report of the activities conducted by the Utah innovation fund and submit, in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(1)(a): the governor;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(1)(b): the Business, Economic Development, and Labor Appropriations Subcommittee;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(1)(c): the Economic Development and Workforce Services Interim Committee; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(1)(d): the Retirement and Independent Entities Interim Committee.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2): 63N-21-402; 63N-21-203(1)(b); 63N-21-201(4)(g); 63N-21-301(2) The annual report shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(a): be designed to provide clear, accurate, and accessible information to the public, the governor, and the Legislature;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(b): 63N-21-402 include a copy of the annual audit required under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(c): 63N-21-203(1)(b) describe the policies adopted by the board under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d): include detailed information regarding:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d)(i): the name and location of each qualified business that received capital from the Utah innovation fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d)(ii): the amount of each qualified investment made by the Utah innovation fund;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d)(iii): the aggregate amount of capital provided to qualified businesses;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d)(iv): realized gains from qualified investments and any realized losses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(d)(v): unrealized gains and any unrealized losses based on the net present value of ongoing qualified investments;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(e): include detailed information regarding the innovation lab's yearly expenditures, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(e)(i): administrative, operating, and financing expenses; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(e)(ii): aggregate compensation information for full-time and part-time employees, including benefit and travel expenses;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(f): 63N-21-201(4)(g) include detailed information regarding all funding sources for administrative, operating, and financing expenses, including any fees charged by the innovation lab to the Utah innovation fund under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-401(2)(g): 63N-21-301(2) include an explanation of the Utah innovation fund's progress in achieving the purposes described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402 Annual audit.
----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(1): Each calendar year, an audit of the activities of the Utah innovation fund shall be conducted by:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(1)(a): the state auditor; or
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(1)(b): an independent auditor engaged by the state auditor.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(2): (1)(b) An independent auditor described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3): 63N-21-401 The annual audit shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3)(a): include a valuation of the assets owned by the Utah innovation fund as of the end of the reporting year, using market-standard techniques for assets typically held by early stage private investment and venture capital funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3)(b): 63N-21-401 include an opinion regarding the accuracy of the information provided in the annual report described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3)(c): on or before September 1, be delivered to:
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3)(c)(i): the innovation lab; and
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(3)(c)(ii): the state treasurer.
Utah Code Annotated § 63N-21-402(4): The innovation lab shall pay the costs associated with the annual audit.
